### [204] [BORA: Bridging Offline Reinforcement Learning and Online Residual Adaptation for Real-World Dexterous VLA Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30226)
*Zhongxi Chen,Yifan Han,Yanming Shao,Huanming Liu,Congsheng Xu,Xiaoyu Chen,Yao Mu,Wenzhao Lian*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了BORA框架，通过离线到在线的强化学习后训练，提升了视觉-语言-动作(VLA)模型在真实世界高维灵巧操作任务中的表现，有效提升了任务成功率和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视觉-语言-动作(VLA)模型在对机器人进行真实世界中的高维灵巧操作时，由于手部控制维度高和执行误差累积，导致动作生成与物理执行之间存在明显差距。而现有的强化学习后训练又面临样本效率低、时序不一致和硬件风险高等问题。因此，需要一种新颖高效且安全的训练机制。

Method: 作者提出了BORA框架。离线阶段，利用视觉语言模型（VLM）的认知表达和动作片段，训练可进行动作条件价值引导的评论器。在线阶段，冻结VLA主网络，引入低成本、人工介入的人在回路残差自适应机制，实时修正物理环境下的执行误差，通过继承的评论器和基于干预的奖励信号，纠正实际执行和离线学习目标的偏差。

Result: 在五个复杂真实灵巧操作任务上的实验表明，BORA相比纯行为克隆和传统解耦强化学习方法，平均成功率提升33%，在新物体泛化任务中，最大提升达到43%。

Conclusion: BORA框架有效弥合了视觉语言动作模型的感知-执行鸿沟，显著提升了机器人在高维真实操作中的表现，对提升通用智能机器人的操控能力具有实际意义。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have emerged as a promising paradigm for grounding visual-language understanding into real-world robotic manipulation. However, dexterous manipulation remains challenging for VLA policies due to high-dimensional hand control and compounding execution errors, which makes real-world RL post-training essential for bridging the gap between visually grounded action generation and physically reliable dexterous execution. However, high-dimensional dexterous exploration often triggers temporal inconsistency, sample inefficiency and hardware risks in the real world. To address these challenges, we propose BORA, an offline-to-online RL post-training framework designed for real-world dexterous VLA models. In the offline phase, BORA constructs a critic that takes both the VLM's cognition tokens and action chunks as inputs. This design enables action-conditioned value guidance, allowing the critic to evaluate dexterous hand motions beyond visual context alone. During the subsequent online phase, BORA freezes the VLA base and introduces a lightweight, Human-in-the-Loop (HiL) chunk-wise residual adaptation mechanism to mitigate real-world execution errors and further correct the offline-learned intents within the actual physical environment. By inheriting the offline critic and employing intervention-driven rewards, BORA effectively corrects execution discrepancies and adapts to real-world physical variances while preserving the pretrained policy as a stable prior. Extensive evaluations across five complex real-world dexterous tasks demonstrate that BORA significantly outperforms pure imitation learning and traditional decoupled RL baselines, achieving a 33% absolute increase in average success rate under standard settings and up to a 43% improvement in unseen object generalization.

Experiments on manipulation, navigation, and trajectory-centric benchmarks show consistent multi-task performance and out-of-distribution generalization under variations in scene layout, background, lighting, object configuration, and robot embodiment. Method: 框架通过跨视角语义匹配将第一人称注视点映射到机器人观察视角，生成目标物体掩码和注视点，实现从粗到细的目标指定。随后，这些注视线索以感知级提示和动作级调控的方式融入机器人策略中，使机器人精确聚焦与执行复杂操作。

To address this limitation, we propose Gaze2Act, a novel VLA framework that leverages human gaze as a dynamic and intuitive intent signal for complex interactive manipulation. These cues are then integrated into the policy through perception-level prompting and action-level conditioning, allowing the robot to attend to relevant regions and execute precise interactions under dynamic intent. ### [207] [A Heterogeneous Architecture for Robot RL Beyond GPU-Dominant Paradigms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30313)
*Yufei Jia,Zhanxiang Cao,Mingrui Yu,Heng Zhang,Shenyu Chen,Dixuan Jiang,Meng Li,Xiaofan Li,Yiyang Liu,Junzhe Wu,Zheng Li,XiLin Fang,Tingyu Cui,Shengcheng Fu,Haoyang Li,Anqi Wang,Zifan Wang,Dongjie Zhu,Chenyu Cao,Zhenbiao Huang,Ziang Zheng,Jie Lu,Xin Ma,Zhengyang Wei,Xiang Zhao,Tianyue Zhan,Ye He,Yuxiang Chen,Yizhou Jiang,Yue Li,Haizhou Ge,Yuhang Dong,Fan Jia,Ziheng Zhang,Meng Zhang,Xiwa Deng,Zhixing Chen,Hanyang Shao,Chenxin Dong,Yixuan Li,Yizhi Chen,Bokui Chen,Kaifeng Zhang,Hanqing Cui,Yusen Qin,Ruqi Huang,Lei Han,Tiancai Wang,Xiang Li,Yue Gao,Guyue Zhou*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出并实现了UniLab，一个异构CPU模拟和GPU学习混合架构，在机器人强化学习中显著提升了训练效率，并破除了物理仿真必须在GPU上运行的常规认知，同时实现了更好的跨平台兼容性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前机器人强化学习的主流做法倾向于将物理仿真、策略采样和模型学习全部集成在GPU上，获得了极高的训练效率。但这种范式固化了“高效训练需依赖GPU物理引擎”的观念，限制了系统设计和平台兼容性。作者希望挑战这一假设，探索是否存在更灵活、同样高效的方案。

Method: 作者提出UniLab架构，将仿真阶段充分并行化后放在CPU端，而模型学习留在GPU端，通过高效的运行时系统实现数据传输、缓存和同步的统一管理。系统支持多种主流强化学习算法，并通过CPU批量物理引擎达成高仿真吞吐量。

Result: 在多种典型的机器人控制任务上，UniLab在相同硬件条件下实现了3到10倍的端到端训练效率提升，且显著降低了对NVIDIA CUDA栈的依赖，可在Apple macOS、AMD ROCm和Intel XPU等多平台运行。

Conclusion: 高效的训练过程不一定要求物理仿真必须在GPU上进行，CPU并行模拟结合高效的数据通路同样能够实现高效训练。UniLab丰富了机器人强化学习系统的设计空间，为实际部署和平台兼容性提供了更多选择。

Abstract: Simulation-based RL for contemporary robot control is increasingly organized around GPU-resident simulation: physics, rollout collection, and learning are placed on a single GPU-centric execution path. This paradigm has greatly improved training speed, but it has also encouraged a default assumption that efficient training requires physics to reside on the GPU. We revisit this assumption. Our view is that, in simulation-dominated robot control, the essential question is not which processor runs physics, but whether simulation throughput, policy learning, and runtime synchronization form an efficient end-to-end loop. We present UniLab, a heterogeneous CPU-simulation / GPU-learning architecture that decouples CPU-parallel simulation from GPU policy updates through a unified runtime for data movement, buffering, and synchronization. UniLab is implemented as a complete and extensible training system using MuJoCoUni and MotrixSim CPU-batched physics backends, supporting PPO, SAC, FlashSAC, TD3, and APPO. On representative simulation-based robot control tasks, UniLab improves end-to-end training efficiency by 3--10$\times$ under the same hardware configuration, while reducing dependence on the NVIDIA CUDA-based software stack and supporting cross-platform execution on the Apple macOS platform and the AMD ROCm and Intel XPU accelerator backends. These results show that GPU simulation is an effective path to efficient training, but not a necessary one, broadening the practical system choices available for robot RL training. Project page: https://github.com/unilabsim/UniLab.

</details>


### [208] [RoboWits: Unexpected Challenges for Robotic Creative Problem Solving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30326)
*Chunru Lin,Hongxin Zhang,Fenghao Yu,Zhehuan Chen,Thomas L. Griffiths,Yejin Choi,David Held,Chuang Gan*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了RoboWits，一个用于系统性评估机器人认知推理、创造性工具使用和应对突发状况能力的双机械臂基准测试体系，并开发了自动化任务生成流程用于构建高质量的智能推理场景。实验结果显示，当前主流机器人政策在应对突发变化和复杂推理任务方面表现有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人评测大多注重动作执行能力，缺乏对认知推理和应变能力的系统性评估，而这些能力对真实环境机器人应用至关重要。

Method: 提出了RoboWits基准，包括30个种子任务和208个经过变化和分级难度设计的任务，涵盖几何、材料和装配推理。为任务构建，开发了多智能体协作的自动化流程，包括任务生成、验证、指标与场景生成和任务变异。

Result: 主流的预训练视觉语言代理（VLA）在单任务微调后可在种子任务上取得初步成功，但在变异任务上的表现显著下降，反映出现有方法在面对复杂推理和环境变化时的脆弱性。

Conclusion: RoboWits有效揭示了机器人在复杂认知推理和适应性任务中的短板，有助推动该领域算法和模型的进一步研究与发展。

Abstract: The ability to reason, adapt, and creatively solve problems under unexpected challenges is essential for robots operating in real-world environments. However, current robotic benchmarks primarily emphasize skill-level execution and provide limited insight into such cognitive reasoning capabilities. We introduce RoboWits, a bi-manual robotic benchmark designed to systematically evaluate cognitive reasoning, creative tool use, and robustness to unexpected conditions. To enable scalable construction of high-quality reasoning-centric unexpected scenarios, we propose an automated task generation pipeline formulated as a multi-agent cooperative framework, comprising agents for seed task generation and verification, metric generation, scene generation, and task mutation. Using the pipeline, we curated 30 diverse seed tasks and 208 tasks with mutations and graded difficulty across geometry, material, and assembly-based reasoning. We benchmark popular robot policies, pre-trained VLAs, and oracle-state planners. Our results reveal a significant performance gap: while pre-trained VLAs exhibit preliminary success on seed tasks after single-task fine-tuning, they struggle to perform on mutated tasks, implying their brittleness in manipulation tasks requiring reasoning, strategy adaptation, and robustness to deceptive or constrained environments. Project page is available at https://umass-embodied-agi.github.io/RoboWits.

</details>


### [209] [DynaFLIP: Rethinking Robotics Perception via Tri-Modal-Dynamics Guided Representation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30350)
*Jusuk Lee,Seungjae Lee,Jonghun Shin,Hoseong Jung,Sungha Kim,Daesol Cho,H. Jin Kim,Jia-Bin Huang,Furong Huang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出DynaFLIP，一个动态感知的多模态预训练框架，通过图像、语言和3D流数据联合训练，使视觉编码器更好地理解动作相关的场景动态性，从而提升机器人操控能力，实验在多种仿真与真实场景下均优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人学习系统大多基于为静态识别或视觉-语言任务预训练的视觉编码器，而忽略了动作和动态理解，这限制了操控泛化能力。为提升感知对操控关键动态信息的编码能力，有必要推动动态理解从下游决策上移到感知模块。

Method: 构建来自人类及机器人视频的图像、语言、3D流三元组作为训练监督，设计多模态编码器，采取极小Simplex体积损失、余弦正则和对比损失，促进三模态特征高度对齐且避免几何退化，从而推动感知端学习动作相关区域的动态表征。

Result: DynaFLIP生成的动态感知视觉特征在多种下游策略（含视觉-语言代理）中效果明显优于基线方法，泛化性强，特别是在分布外任务提升达22.5%。同时分析表明其关注于对操控关键的感知区域。

Conclusion: 动态感知预训练能极大提升机器人视觉表征的泛化及操控性能，建议未来视觉表征除关注物体是什么，还需编码其随动作变化的动态特征。

Abstract: Robot manipulation critically depends on perception that preserves the action-relevant aspects of a scene. Yet most robot learning pipelines are built upon visual encoders pre-trained for static recognition or vision-language alignment, leaving motion understanding to downstream policies. We introduce DynaFLIP, a dynamics-aware multimodal pre-training framework that pushes motion understanding upstream into perception. We construct image-language-3D flow triplets from heterogeneous human and robot videos, and use these triplets as training-time supervision to shape an image-only encoder. Our key idea is to encourage the three modalities to span a small simplex volume in the shared hyperspherical space -- a smaller simplex volume indicating stronger alignment. To avoid the geometric ambiguity and trivial collapse of naive volume minimization, we combine simplex-volume minimization with a cosine regularizer and a contrastive objective. Our analyses show that DynaFLIP focuses on control-relevant regions critical for manipulation. The resulting dynamics-aware representations serve as reusable visual backbones and consistently outperform baselines across diverse downstream policies, including VLAs. We validate this across diverse simulation and real-world setups, with gains reaching +22.5% under out-of-distribution scenarios. Our results suggest that robot generalization improves when visual representations are trained to encode not just what is present, but how the world changes under action.

</details>
